-   Security implication 13 including encryption, isolation, and
    compliance aspects for Future Enhancements.
-   Observability & monitoring note 13 describing metrics, logs, and
    tracing for Future Enhancements.
-   Detailed specification point 14 for Future Enhancements.
-   Implementation detail 14 covering edge cases, constraints,
    validations, and scalability for Future Enhancements.
-   Configuration standard 14 including environment variables,
    deployment strategy, and performance considerations for Future
    Enhancements.
-   Security implication 14 including encryption, isolation, and
    compliance aspects for Future Enhancements.
-   Observability & monitoring note 14 describing metrics, logs, and
    tracing for Future Enhancements.
-   Detailed specification point 15 for Future Enhancements.
-   Implementation detail 15 covering edge cases, constraints,
    validations, and scalability for Future Enhancements.

# Architecture Diagrams

``` mermaid
flowchart TD
A[Client] --> B[API Gateway]
B --> C[RFP Service]
B --> D[NLP Service]
B --> E[Estimation Service]
E --> F[ML Model Service]
D --> G[LLM Provider]
F --> H[Model Registry]
```

``` mermaid
erDiagram
ORGANIZATION ||--o{ USER : has
ORGANIZATION ||--o{ RFP : owns
RFP ||--o{ REQUIREMENT : contains
REQUIREMENT ||--o{ MODULE : maps_to
MODULE ||--o{ TASK : breaks_into
TASK ||--|| EFFORT_ESTIMATE : produces
```

``` mermaid
sequenceDiagram
User->>API: Upload RFP
API->>NLP: Extract Requirements
NLP->>LLM: Parse Document
LLM-->>NLP: Structured JSON
NLP->>Estimation: Generate Effort
Estimation-->>User: Estimation Result
```
